German Warship Emden to Visit China 93

Expected to Arrive in Shanghai on the 21st of Next Month. It is reported that the German warship Emden is about to visit China. The ship is scheduled to sail from the Philippines on April 15 and arrive in Nanjing. It will be berthed in Nanjing until April 20, and then arrive in Shanghai around April 21. It will stay in Shanghai for about a week. The German Navy has named its warships Emden three times, and the current ship is its third one. It has been learned that the Emden was launched on January 7, 1925, and officially joined the Navy on October 15 of the same year. It has a displacement of 6,000 tons, a length of 155 meters, a width of 14.03 meters, and a draft of 6.03 meters. The ship has 22 officers, 3 warrant officers, 15 lieutenants, 112 sergeants, 314 soldiers, and 67 naval cadets. The ship is equipped with eight 15 cm guns, two 8.8 cm guns, and two surface torpedo tubes. Its maximum speed is 29.05 nautical miles per hour. The ship served as a training ship from 1926 to 1928 and from 1928 to 1929, circumnavigating the globe twice. In the spring of 1930, it also made a four-month overseas voyage in the West Indian Ocean. The ship will now sail overseas for twelve months, passing through the Mediterranean Sea, the Indian Ocean, and East Asia, and then returning via Africa. The main purpose of this voyage of the German ship Emden is to train naval cadets and officers and men on board. The ship carries a total of 67 naval officers, machinists, and quartermasters who are in training. They have received six months of training in their own country before this overseas voyage. After the voyage is completed at the end of December this year, they will take the entrance examination. The captain of the Emden is Lieutenant Commander Witthoef. During the European War in 1914, Witthoef served as the torpedo officer on the German warship Emden. Witthoef personally participated in all the battles fought by the former Emden in the Indian Ocean at that time. The executive officer of the ship is Lieutenant Commander Siemens. Siemens served in the German First High Seas Cruiser Squadron during the European War from 1914 to 1918. The chief engineer of the ship, Lieutenant Commander Kaufmadn, also served in the German First High Seas Cruiser Squadron at the beginning of the European War and served as the chief engineer of the submarine force in the Mediterranean Sea from 1916 to 1918. The ship's press officer is Lieutenant Commander Ltiele. It is said that the captain of the ship will also entertain journalists. The date will be determined after arrival in Shanghai.

Scheduled for Full Handover Today　　Social Affairs Bureau Sends Personnel to Investigate Thoroughly. Sanxin Textile Co., Ltd. has more than 4,000 male and female workers, registered in Hong Kong under the British merchant brand. The factory owner is Sheng Xuanhuai. After Xuanhuai's death, his sons Sheng Zecheng, Sheng Pingcheng, and Sheng Shengzu continued to manage it. The manager is Sheng Yulin. It is not yet clear to the outside world whether this sale is to Japanese or Chinese.

Authorities Investigate Thoroughly. All the workers of the Sanxin Textile Factory were informed that the factory was to be sold and handed over. Therefore, they specially elected representatives Hou Jia Hai, Lou Tai Zhong, Gu Lan Sheng, etc. yesterday afternoon to submit a petition to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, requesting assistance. After receiving the report, the bureau believed that it was a major issue concerning the future of China's textile industry. Petition from the Workers' Union. The Textile Industry Workers' Union of the Third Special District submitted a document to the Social Affairs Bureau yesterday, stating that the Sanxin Yarn Factory has announced its sale and that the entire factory must be handed over tomorrow (i.e., the 19th). Please provide assistance. It is thought that the factory is not failing in business and is not going bankrupt, but it is causing all 4,000 workers of the union to have nowhere to seek food and to be buried in a dead end. Some of the workers have been working in the factory since childhood and are now old and exhausted. They have made some contributions to the factory. Now, the union has submitted a request on behalf of all the workers, requesting your bureau to find a way to provide assistance and negotiate for compensation. The undersigned is fearful and awaits orders. Sincerely submitted.

Member Representatives of Trade Associations Representing Two Types of Firms 95

Interpretation by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter from the Silk and Satin Industry Consolidation Committee, inquiring whether there should be restrictions on the member representatives of trade associations representing two types of firms. It had previously submitted a request to the Social Affairs Bureau for interpretation. Now, the bureau has forwarded the Supreme Court's interpretation to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to inform the association that for companies and firms that send representatives to attend the association, each company and firm may send one to two people, limited to managers or principals. If a firm has two locations, both of which are personally operated and have no other managers or principals who can represent them, then one person can represent both firms. However, non-profit legal persons are different from for-profit legal persons. Therefore, they can only exercise one voting right or right to vote.

Important Shipping News 98

Tonghua Collides. The Tonghua, a coastal steamer of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, was berthed at the Dapu Wharf in Haizhou to unload cargo. At that time, the Xuzhou, a steamer of the United States Company, also arrived at the site. Due to excessive tides, the Xuzhou's hull crashed into the Tonghua. At this time, the Tonghua was berthed at the wharf and could not retreat, but it was above the waterline and did not affect navigation. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has already telegraphed the Tonghua to return to Shanghai and send personnel to inspect and claim compensation from the United States Company after clarifying the extent of the damage and estimating the repair costs. There were no losses to passengers or cargo.

Reef Discovered. The Gongping, a steamer of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, sailed to Dalian. The first batch of 22 navigation school students in the bureau were assigned to the ship for practice. According to the ship's telegraph yesterday, a new reef was discovered near Sheshan, ninety nautical miles away. It was not marked on the nautical chart, but it is a necessary route for Qingdao Haizhou navigation. All Qinghai ships must pay extra attention to this new reef when traveling to and from Qinghai. Stamp Duty on Tickets. The Shanghai Shipping Association specially invited representatives of various shipping companies to a meeting to discuss the issue of affixing stamp duty to ship tickets. They unanimously opposed it and decided to reply to the municipal government later.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Abolishes the Foreign Crew Pension System 99

Abolishing Unilateral Unequal Demands　　Newly Revised Regulations for Rewarding and Commiserating with Crew Members　　General Manager Li Explained to Foreign Staff Yesterday. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company still has more than thirty foreign crew members, most of whom have served for two or three years. Since the last case of Jiang'an Chief Mate Keranek requesting retirement and pension, the lawsuit has lasted for more than a year, and the result was rejected by the court. Other British crew members who have retired and demanded pensions from the bureau and the British Minister to China have raised negotiations. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company also discussed a solution to this case. After the Airin ship was sunk by British artillery off the coast of Huizhou, the responsibility for compensation has not yet been resolved. The bureau has replied to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs that the pensions of the retired British crew members can be allocated, but the case of the British warship sinking the Airin ship should also be compensated. The matter can be resolved after the compensation is paid. General Manager Li issued a notice to reward and commiserate with crew members and to provide retirement funds, stating that the treatment of crew members at all levels was rarely regulated when the company was privately run. After the company was nationalized in February of the 17th year, although the dismissal of various crew members seemed to create a regulation, those who had served for many years had no reward. This was not in line with the idea of rewarding hard work. As for the foreign crew members, in 1921, at the beginning of the European War, the foreign crew members in China jointly wrote to Chinese and foreign shipping companies requesting subsidies, retirement pensions, and other extra allowances to prevent foreign crew members from competing in China after the war and to protect their original jobs. At that time, the former directors were suffering from environmental pressure and reluctantly agreed to the request. Now that times have changed, the root cause of this request has long disappeared completely, and Jardine Matheson and Taikoo have also revised their regulations. This one-sided unequal request between Chinese and foreigners has long been invalid in our bureau, and there is no reason to continue it alone. Since taking over the management, former General Manager Zhao issued the crew service regulations, which were very detailed in terms of dividing positions and establishing systems. However, the retirement and pension issues were not regulated, and there were as many as forty to fifty foreign crew members who had served for two and a half years without being handled according to these regulations. This shows that the unequal demands between Chinese and foreigners had long been obvious. The Jiang'an chief mate case is further evidence that this regulation should be abolished. Over the years, no foreign crew member has raised objections, and there has been no written statement from foreign crew members in the previous files. There is no doubt that foreign crew members have tacitly agreed to the abolition. The commissioner cares for workers and treats Chinese and foreigners equally. He expresses his appreciation for the foreign crew members' understanding of the situation and their loyalty to their duties. In addition to the special regulations for crew service, regulations will be promulgated to reward the foreign crew members who serve in the bureau, taking into account the situation of the bureau and reconciling the old and new regulations to formulate simple reward and commiseration regulations to make up for the previous deficiencies. All retirement bonuses for foreign crew members will be in accordance with the regulations in this chapter (omitted below). The reward and commiseration methods are divided into six levels, from five years to more than thirty years, with every five years as a level. At each level, a salary of one month will be given. Those who have served for more than five years and retire will be given a bonus of one month, two months for more than ten years, three months for more than fifteen years, and so on, up to six months. Those who are injured or killed on duty or become disabled will be given a pension according to the circumstances. After the publication of these regulations, some foreign crew members on various ships who did not understand the situation and caused misunderstandings and panic, General Manager Li heard about this yesterday and immediately invited the chief shipowner of the bureau, McKenna, the deputy chief shipowner, and the chief engineer to explain in person. Since the foreign crew members are serving in the bureau and the bureau is state-owned, the staff should abide by Chinese laws and regulations. He also stated that the treatment in the new reward and commiseration regulations is fair and generous. The chief shipowner and others saw it as a consolation for the foreign staff and explained it for them to avoid misunderstandings. This matter is expected to not cause problems.

Third Day's Record of the National Cotton Production Conference 101

Resolved to Establish the China Cotton Production Improvement Association Nationwide Establishment of Cotton Production and Sales Cooperatives Subsidizing Students to Cultivate Specialized Talents The National Cotton Production Improvement Statistics Conference held its third day of meetings yesterday. The meeting began at 9:00 AM with over fifty representatives in attendance. The chairman was Li Guozhen, and the recorders were Chu Xiusheng and Zheng Yunian. First, Jiang Dixian reported on the cotton flowers recommended by the United Yarn Factories Association to various factories over the years. Then, Mr. Fang Junqiang gave a speech on reasonable promotion matters. Subsequently, proposals were discussed. In the afternoon, the entire group visited the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau. The details of each matter are recorded separately below.

Page 10

Resolutions on Various Cases (Case 1) Proposal to Establish the China Cotton Production Improvement Association Resolution: (1) All organizations attending this conference, except for the Ministry of Industry, shall be the initiators. (2) Lu Feizhi, Feng Zhaochuan, Sun Siqing, Ye Yuanding, Wang Zhiqing, and Fang Junqiang are elected as preparatory members to draft the articles of association. Chen Yanshan, Zhang Zongcheng, and Yuan Zhong are elected as alternate preparatory members. (3) Lu Feizhi is elected as the chairman. (4) The draft articles of association shall be submitted to the general assembly for discussion at 1:30 PM on the 19th. (Case 2) Proposal to Guide Farmers in Organizing Cotton Production and Sales Cooperatives Nationwide by the Provincial Agricultural Associations to Increase the Price of High-Quality Cotton to Benefit Cotton Production Improvement Resolution: (1) Organize agricultural cooperatives. (2) For the high-quality cotton sold by cooperatives or the cotton collected by agricultural farms as whole bales, yarn factories should especially increase their prices and provide economic conveniences. (3) Request the National Government to exempt cooperatives and farms that collect cotton from business taxes. (4) After the establishment of the China Cotton Production Improvement Association, negotiate with the Chinese Yarn Factories Association to formulate trial implementation methods. (Case 3) Cultivate Specialized Cotton Industry Talents and Subsidize Overseas Studies Resolution: Adopted in accordance with the review opinions. The review opinions suggest that the National Government instruct the Ministry of Education and the provincial governments of cotton-producing provinces to: (1) Establish special cotton industry quotas when selecting students for overseas study. (2) Subsidize those who have served in cotton research and testing institutions for many years and are qualified to study abroad.

Today's Agenda The meeting will start at 9:00 AM, with Mr. Na As discussing the American cotton production estimation method. The meeting will conclude. The afternoon meeting will start at 1:30 PM, with Zhang Xinyi lecturing on Chinese cotton production statistical methods. After the lecture, there will be a meeting. Tonight at 6:00 PM, Mr. Chen Zi and Mr. Yang Xixian of Hengda Xinlongmao Yarn Factory will host a banquet for the representatives.

Important Speech Yesterday afternoon, when the representatives visited the Commodity Inspection Bureau, Ye Yuanding gave a speech on China's cotton inspection policy and cotton industry improvement issues. His speech stated: Cotton has always been one of China's key agricultural products. The annual production is estimated at approximately seven million dan, and the cotton field area is thirty million mu. Approximately three million farmers rely on cotton cultivation for a living. There are countless millions of others who indirectly rely on the cotton industry and commerce for a living. Therefore, its impact on the national lifeline and people's livelihood is extremely significant. Although China's climate is mild and its soil is fertile, and the area suitable for cotton is even more abundant than in the United States, the results are far apart, which is unexpected. In addition, China's total population accounts for a quarter of the world's population, while cotton production only accounts for one-tenth of the world's production. As a result, more than three million dan of foreign cotton and two hundred million taels of foreign cotton textiles are imported annually. Chinese people must spare no effort to seek improvement. If the cotton industry fails to compete, it will be harmful to the country and the people. There are myriad ways to improve the cotton industry. Except for promoting benefits and eliminating disadvantages, implementing a cotton inspection policy is the primary attempt. China's cotton is prone to water and impurities, especially water, which is the most widespread problem and has been a long-standing practice. Each year, this results in rejection or price suppression in the international market and raw material spoilage and mechanical damage in the domestic market, with a value of approximately several million taels. Moreover, Chinese people are willing to use foreign cotton mixed with impurities as raw materials for spinning, with an annual outflow of approximately ninety million taels. Eliminating the drawbacks of cotton and stopping unnecessary losses is a passive improvement for cotton inspection policies. Furthermore, China's cotton trade has never had a detailed analysis and standardized grading system based on scientific methods. It only uses place names or province names as standards, such as Tongzhou cotton or Shaanxi cotton. However, cotton quality can vary greatly due to environmental influences such as climate, variety, and human labor. If grading and pricing are based on local areas, then low-quality cotton from famous cotton-producing areas can obtain high prices, while high-quality cotton from unknown areas will have the same price as ordinary low-quality cotton. Without scientific standards and grades, merchants can easily profit from this, deliberately lowering prices and causing farmers to suffer endless losses. This cannot stimulate the farmers' competitive spirit. Farmers do not pay attention to variety cultivation improvement. Although the government or private individuals promote improvements, it is difficult to achieve good results because cotton merchants control everything. Farmers exhaust their efforts to harvest high-quality cotton but still cannot obtain the benefits they deserve, so it is better to cultivate low-quality cotton with extensive cultivation. Creating cotton grading standards to protect the interests of cotton farmers is an active improvement for cotton inspection policies. In addition, there are origin publicity, ginning household registration, cotton industry statistics, market reports, packaging ginning research, and storage construction, etc., which not only directly promote the comprehensive cotton inspection policy but also indirectly benefit the cotton industry. Based on the above reasons, the current National Government has made a great determination to eliminate the accumulated drawbacks of the cotton industry in the short term and plans for future development. Cotton inspection bureaus or branches will be established in Shanghai, Hankou, Tianjin, Ningbo, Shashi, Jinan, and other places to strictly inspect and fundamentally eliminate the water issue in cotton within five years. After five years, the water inspection will end, and the government will issue regulations to prevent future troubles. Cotton inspection will focus on research and promotion of grade standards and quality appraisal, so that China's cotton industry will improve day by day and keep pace with the United States, which will not only be a blessing for the country but also benefit cotton industry farmers and merchants.

Various Groups Welcome Zhu Qinglan 102

Assisting in Disaster Relief in Shaanxi With the disaster in Shaanxi becoming increasingly severe, Zhu Ziqiao, Kang Jiyao, and Zha Mianshen came to Shanghai to raise funds for relief. Yesterday afternoon at 5:00 PM, the local Chinese and Foreign Relief Society held a board meeting to welcome the three gentlemen to report on the disaster situation. The Chinese and Western directors hosted the meeting. Chairman Song Hanzhang delivered a speech, saying that everyone in the country knows that Mr. Zhu and Mr. Kang are great philanthropists. This time, they personally investigated the disaster in Shaanxi, braving the wind and dust, and spared no effort to appeal for help. We are greatly honored by their presence at our society. Since the disaster occurred in the northwest, our society has cooperated with the Chinese and Foreign Relief Society in Xi'an to provide relief. At the same time, Henan, Gansu, Shandong, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and other provinces have successively reported famine, and although we have considered all aspects, we have never stopped providing assistance. However, this is only a small part of our duty. The disaster in Shaanxi has lasted for three years, and our society has remitted a total of 268,500 yuan to the Shaanxi Society for relief, which has only been able to increase the number of porridge factories and shelters. We are deeply ashamed that our efforts have been insufficient. Mr. Zhu's efforts to save the disaster victims in Shaanxi are well known to our society and are admirable. Mr. Kang is the chairman of the Shaanxi Chinese and Foreign Relief Society and is also a rare talent in the charity world. In the report from the Shaanxi Society, we learned that Mr. Kang's leadership is well-organized and practical, and that funds are not wasted. Both of them can be regarded as the two major saviors of the Northwest. We are grateful for their visit and guidance, which has benefited all of us. It is a pity that Mr. Zhu has other engagements and cannot stay for a long conversation, which is a regret. I would like to express my sincere welcome in a few words. We also welcome Mr. Zha Mianzheng's presence at our society today. Mr. Zha has always been very enthusiastic about the relief efforts in Shaanxi and admires Mr. Zhu very much. Mr. Zhu stood up and responded with (1) thanks for the relief, (2) a report on the disaster situation, and (3) a request for all charitable organizations to achieve the goal of saving people in the serious disaster in Shaanxi. At this critical time, with only three months left until the wheat harvest, emergency relief is important, but work relief must also be considered. We hope to raise more relief funds to complete the charitable cause and hope that the government will assist in forming a large organization to work together. Because the disaster area is too large, it will not be effective without this. Mr. Kang said that the disaster in Shaanxi is so tragic that words cannot describe it. There are more than three million dead and more than ten thousand unburied bodies. This is a true fact. The reason why they have not been buried is that most of their families have died. Recently, two Western officials inspected the disaster area and said that they had never seen or heard of such a thing. The disaster in Fufeng and other counties is particularly severe. The funds recently remitted by the Shanghai Society have been used to establish six more shelters, but there are still at least two months before the wheat harvest. In these two months, each person needs at least two yuan in relief to save a life. If we do not actively provide relief at this time, it will be a waste of effort. Mr. Zhang Xianqing then described the situation of personally providing relief in Shaanxi, saying that it is difficult to achieve a thorough solution without work relief, but work relief requires a large amount of relief funds. The Chinese and Western directors were deeply moved and hoped that all sectors of society would assist in completing the charitable cause.

Ningbo-Shaoxing Fellow Association The Ningbo Fellow Association and the Shaoxing Fellow Association in Shanghai held a banquet yesterday afternoon at the Fellow Association Hall to welcome Zhu Qinglan. During the banquet, Zhu Qinglan reported on the disaster situation in Shaanxi, hoping that Ningbo and Shaoxing and people in Shanghai would assist in providing relief so that the survivors of the disaster could survive. Everyone present was moved. At the end of the banquet, a film about the Shaanxi disaster was shown before the gathering dispersed.

Yang Zuorong Appeals for the People of Gansu Province 104

Sending letters to various groups to beg for aid, the representative of the Gansu Accounts Committee, Yang Zuorong, yesterday sent letters to various groups reporting on the disaster situation in Gansu. He stated that Gansu is located in a remote area in the west, with poor transportation, and has suffered a great calamity for five years. Because the people have been under the long-standing intimidation of Feng's troops, it is difficult for them to speak out. The accountants are unable to move forward due to dangerous roads, so the true situation of the disaster in Gansu has not been fully disclosed, which is very painful. The disaster situation is described as follows: 1. Drought: The autumn harvest in the sixteenth year was poor, there was no harvest in the seventeenth year, the harvest in the eighteenth year was less than 20%, and there was no ability to plant in the nineteenth year. More than one million people have died of starvation in the 60 disaster-stricken counties. 2. War: In the five years since Feng's troops entered Gansu, they have forcibly conscripted 200,000 soldiers and ordered the counties to forcibly requisition military vehicles and horses, as well as apportion funds and grain. 3. Banditry: Within three years, more than 200,000 people throughout the province have died directly at the hands of bandits. Houses have been burned, and women have been looted in every county. Villages have been reduced to ruins, and fields have been abandoned. There is no plan for relief. There are only survivors who hope to provide assistance.

Taxpayers Association Protests the Municipal Council's Assessment of Donations 107

Letter Requesting Cancellation Notification Not to Pay Official Letter from the Chinese Ratepayers' Association According to a report from the China Chemical Industry Society on Henan Road, the association sent another letter to the Municipal Council, stating: "We are writing to inform you that the basis for the municipal general donation (巡捕捐) is the actual rent, in addition to the estimated rent for self-owned properties, which is the principle of municipal finance. We requested your bureau to pay attention to this matter in our letter of March 6. According to a letter from the Shanghai China Chemical Industry Society, the donation office of the Public Concession Municipal Council notified us on December 22 last year that the annual rent for the properties at 444 and 445 Henan Road, currently occupied by our company, should be increased from 1,666 yuan to 3,162 yuan, and that donation taxes should be collected according to the new amount starting from January 1, 1931. Those who wish to protest should submit a letter within fourteen days from the date of this notification. Since our company's current rent is leased from the accounting department of Thiele & Co. at a monthly rent of 100 taels per building, and we hold a rent receipt as proof, which is 16 taels more expensive than the neighbor's monthly rent of 84 taels, how can it be arbitrarily increased to double the amount? Furthermore, the estimated rent has only been applied to self-owned property owners in the past. Now, an illegal additional burden is suddenly imposed on tenants. Our company cannot recognize this and has already protested within the specified time limit. All the policies of the bureau should be guided by the public opinion of the taxpayers. How can we rashly change precedents? Your association is the largest organization of Chinese taxpayers, and everyone admires your upholding of justice. Our company does not want to set a bad precedent for ourselves and cause unlimited trouble for the entire community in the future. Therefore, we report the facts and send our company's employee, Wu Xiongxiang, to present the details in person. We sincerely ask for your guidance and fairness." Various evidences were also presented to the meeting. After research by the association, it was learned that the Municipal Council's collection of the municipal general donation (also known as the patrol donation) will be calculated based on the estimated rent instead of the actual rent. This method is absolutely considered inappropriate by the association and should be cancelled. Assuming that the actual rent is 100 yuan per month, the total donation will be 14 yuan according to the current rate of 14%. If it is calculated based on the estimated rent, and the estimated rent is 10,000 yuan per month, then the total donation will be 1,400 yuan according to the current rate of 14%. Is this a reasonable method? Calculating according to this case, the estimated rent is almost doubled compared to the actual rent. Isn't the donation rate increased from 14% to 26.57% or more? Therefore, the municipal general donation must not be calculated according to the estimated rent and should be calculated according to the actual rent. Moreover, raising the rent greatly affects the market. According to the above, we hereby send a letter hoping that you will investigate and cancel the unreasonable method of collecting the total donation based on the estimated rent.

Notification The Shanghai Concession Chinese Ratepayers' Association issued a notification yesterday, stating: "For the matter of notification, taxpayers have repeatedly reported that the Municipal Council in the concession will calculate the municipal general donation (i.e., patrol donation) based on the estimated rent instead of the actual rent and has notified that it will be implemented starting from January 1 this year, requesting negotiations, etc., to the association. After investigation, the collection of the municipal general donation based on the actual rent is the practice in this concession and is also the principle of municipal finance. Therefore, the total donation is based on the rent receipt, and only houses that are self-owned and self-occupied and have no rent will be calculated according to the estimated rent. Now, if we, the taxpayers who rent houses, allow the Municipal Council to collect the total donation based on the estimated rent, and the estimated amount of the current Municipal Council is higher than the actual rent, there will inevitably be a day when the total donation exceeds the rent amount, and it will also help to increase the rent and increase the burden. How can taxpayers allow this? In addition to sending a letter to the Municipal Council to cancel this unreasonable method, we hereby notify the taxpayers in the concession that the payment of the total donation should be calculated according to the actual rent and should not be calculated according to the estimated rent. This is a notification from the Shanghai Concession Chinese Ratepayers' Association on March 18, 1931."

Rickshaw Merchants Petitioned Party and Government Agencies Yesterday 108

The Citizens' Training Council Approved No Discussion Because the municipal government is planning to increase the number of rickshaw licenses, rickshaw merchants in the Chinese area jointly petitioned the municipal party headquarters yesterday morning for assistance. About 400 merchants from the northern and southern cities arrived and elected Wang Rongqing, Li Bingyi, Che Lisheng, Zhou Jinting, Yu Dajin, Zhao Tianyuan, and Han Xueyue as petition representatives. The Shanghai Rickshaw Trade Association drafted a petition stating the reasons for the petition. Zhu Ya, the secretary of the Citizens' Training Council, received the delegation. Committee member Wu Kaixian then summoned the representatives to inquire about everything. The representatives immediately stated that the rickshaw industry is difficult and that the rickshaw dealers intend to sabotage the situation. Committee member Wu said that the government's increase in the number of rickshaws is naturally intended to provide for the poor coolies. As for how to increase the number of rickshaws without being deceived by the rickshaw dealers and affecting the livelihoods of the poor, he agreed to forward the intentions to the municipal government. The representatives were all satisfied and returned to the Social Affairs Bureau to petition. Section Chief Tian Heqing received them and agreed to forward the matter to the director and request the municipal government to pay attention to the method of increasing the number of rickshaws. The representatives then dispersed.

Yesterday, the Citizens' Training Council of the Municipal Party Headquarters approved the Shanghai Rickshaw Trade Association's petition, stating: "We have received your petition. The municipal government's increase in the number of rickshaw licenses is originally intended to provide for the poor rickshaw pullers. Your association should uphold this intention to alleviate the hardship of the workers. We fear that unscrupulous merchants may attempt to manipulate the situation. In addition to forwarding a letter from our association to the municipal government to prevent this, your association should pay attention at all times. If you discover the above-mentioned situation, you can report it directly to the association for investigation. The request to cancel the increase in the number of rickshaw licenses should not be discussed."

Store Clerks and Workers Joining Trade Unions 111

The Social Affairs Bureau Promulgates Remedial Measures The Social Affairs Bureau has promulgated a notice on the remedial measures for store clerks and workers to join trade associations. The notice states: "For the matter of the notice, the Municipal Government's No. 7610 instruction has been received, approving the Ministry of Industry's consultation with the Training Department of the Central Executive Committee on the proposed remedial measures for store clerks and workers in various places to join trade associations. The measures are hereby promulgated for compliance by all industries and businesses in the city. The measures are as follows: 1. Amend Article 10 of the Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the Trade Association Law for Industries and Businesses to read: 'The member representatives of each company or store mentioned in Article 7 of this Law shall be limited to one or two persons, who shall be managers or principals. If the average number of store clerks in the most recent year exceeds ten, one additional representative shall be added, who shall be mutually elected by the store clerks of the company or store, but shall not exceed three persons at most.' 2. If store clerks and workers need to request employers to improve their treatment due to factual needs, they may jointly submit a request to the local party and government agencies for mediation. 3. All conditions that have been signed between store clerks and workers in various industries and the respective capital parties shall be re-examined by the local party and government agencies and protected. Those that violate current laws and regulations shall be ordered to be cancelled jointly."

The Strike in Five Silk Factories in Zhabei Resolved 112

Because the capital party stopped providing food to the employees during the shutdown period, which led to a labor strike, the Social Affairs Bureau convened a mediation. Due to the insistence of both labor and capital, no results were achieved. Yesterday, the Zhabei District Silk Factory Workers' Union sent members to negotiate with the factory owners and resolved the matter. The clauses of the settlement agreement are as follows:

The Settlement Agreement of Hengda and Others The Settlement Agreement of Hengda, Jushun, and Jiulun Silk Factories: 1. The factory will compensate for the two months of food that was stopped during the shutdown period, with 10 yuan per person. 2. The salary for five days of work in February will be calculated as the salary for the entire month. 3. The factory's treatment in the future will still be handled according to custom. The above settlement agreement cannot be used as a permanent basis.

The Settlement Agreement of Jintai and Others The Settlement Agreement of Jintai and Zhenhe Silk Factories: 1. The factory will compensate for one month's salary for the two months of the shutdown period. 2. The salary for seven days of work in February will be calculated as half a month's salary. 3. This time, the factory's business has been particularly affected. The treatment of employees in the future will still be handled according to custom.

The Bureau of Works Does Not Purchase the Dahua Hotel 117

Dog Racing Members' Competition Also Not Permitted. The Public Concession Bureau of Works had previously resolved to prohibit the Mingyuan and Shenyuan dog racing tracks within the concession after March 11th. Subsequently, the Mingyuan side changed its approach, advocating for limiting dog racing to members' competitions with the nature of an association, hoping to maintain its disguised gambling. The Board of Directors of the Bureau of Works held a routine meeting yesterday afternoon to discuss the so-called members' competition of Mingyuan and resolved to maintain the original plan. The Mingyuan and Shenyuan dog racing tracks will still be closed at the end of this month, and the so-called members' competition is also not permitted. In addition, the purchase of the Dahua Hotel was also discussed. Because the selling price required 4,111,510 taels, which was too expensive, it was rejected. As for the Bureau of Works adding Chinese to serve as senior staff, the names previously debated included "Chief Chinese Affairs Officer," "Deputy Chief Chinese Affairs Officer," and "Chinese Political Advisor." Another Dispute and Lawsuit Regarding the Sichuan-Hankou Railway 119

Three People Claim to Be General Manager　　Who Is the Real One? Zhang Taijie, the former general manager and resident manager in Hankou of the Sichuan Railway Company, was sued in the Shanghai District Court by Kang Qianli, chairman of the board of directors, on behalf of Zeng Xianzhi, for embezzling more than three million yuan in public funds and sentenced to imprisonment. Since then, many people have been vying for the position of general manager. First, Feng Lizhou and Zou Yunchun, were appointed as acting general manager and resident manager in Hankou, but Feng and Zou did not formally take office for a long time. Chairman Kang Qianli then appointed Ni Gongwei to replace Feng and Zou, while also dismissing Feng and Zou. However, Feng and Zou still demanded reinstatement, leading to disputes, mutual accusations, and the engagement of lawyers to publish notices in newspapers. On February 6th of this year, lawyer Liu Hui, representing Feng and Zou, published an advertisement in the Shen and Xin newspapers, stating that Ni Gongwei's appointment as general manager of the Sichuan Railway Company was a private appointment by Zeng Xianzhi, who had stolen the board of directors' seal, and claiming that Ni Gongwei was attempting to achieve the purpose of accumulating wealth in collusion with Zeng Xianzhi. When Ni saw the advertisement, he believed that his position had been appointed by a majority of the board of directors, while Feng and Zou had been dismissed and were falsely accusing others. He then hired a lawyer to sue Feng and Zou for the crimes of forging documents, defaming reputation and credit, obstructing freedom, and embezzlement under Articles 225, Section 1, 328, 319, and 356 of the Criminal Code. Feng also hired lawyers such as Tang Mingshi to argue that the defendants' publication of the notice was a good-faith expression of opinion and self-defense, which should not be punished according to law, and filed a counterclaim, requesting that Ni be prosecuted for false accusation, fraud, and embezzlement under Articles 180 and 356 of the Criminal Code. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Xiao Xiexun of the Special Court held a hearing. When asked about their professions, the original and defendant both claimed to be the general manager and resident manager in Hankou of the Sichuan Railway Company. The defendant's attorney then stated that the circumstances of the case were very complicated, with many side issues. There are now Sichuan officials and gentry who have come forward as third parties to mediate. If mediation is possible, all lawsuits of the Sichuan Railway Company can be resolved, and this case is related to the case of Feng Lizhou suing Zeng yesterday. The court has already issued an order for Feng's lawsuit against Zeng to be settled out of court (this case was detailed in yesterday's newspaper). Therefore, the defense attorney requested a postponement to attempt mediation, wondering what the plaintiff's attorney thought. The plaintiff's attorney then stated that the plaintiff strongly supports mediation. However, according to Ni Gongwei's opinion, mediation is permissible, but litigation should still proceed. Judge Xiao then declared that the court had previously investigated the Zhang Taijie case at the Shanghai District Court but had not yet received a reply. The witness Liu Yajue and others had also not arrived today, and the three plaintiffs and defendants all claimed to be the general manager and resident manager in Hankou of the Sichuan Railway Company, so it was necessary to investigate to determine who was who. Therefore, the case was adjourned for two weeks for further hearing.

Liu Xieyu, a Student at the Construction University, Imprisoned Due to Friends 120

Two Classmates Suspected of Being Reactionaries　　Liu Also Inevitably Caught in the Whirlpool. Liu Xieyu, a student at the Construction University, is just a young man from Changzhou. He studied at sea, not boarding at the school with other out-of-town students, but renting an apartment near the school at No. 138 Huade Road, Yangshupu. The other day, detectives from the Municipal Public Security Bureau, accompanied by Lee Lian-chuan, an investigator from the Huishan Police Station in charge of the area, suddenly arrested him from his residence. His bedroom was searched and a card with the name Bao Kaizhi and a note with Bao's communication address were found. Bao used to be a classmate of Liu's and was arrested by the Municipal Public Security Bureau with Yang Hongxun on suspicion of being a reactionary. Yang was also Liu's classmate, so he was implicated. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the District Court of the Special Region, where Judge Feng Shide interrogated him. According to the police lawyer Li Zhishan, the card and the note with the communication address were common social items. One should not be considered an accomplice just because the person on the card is a criminal. Therefore, if it is desired to accuse Liu of being a reactionary, concrete evidence must be presented to prove it, otherwise, there is no objection to the Public Security Bureau's request for transfer and interrogation. Otherwise, a postponement should be requested for detailed investigation. Liu Xieyu then testified that although he used to be classmates with Yang and Bao, he had not seen them for a long time. He was unaware of their recent actions and did not know anything about them. Fu Sucun, a detective from the Municipal Public Security Bureau, then stated that Yang and Bao had already been sent to the Garrison Headquarters, so they could not be brought to the court today for questioning. Judge Feng then instructed the defendant Liu Xieyu to be temporarily detained at the police station and adjourned the case for seven days, pending the Municipal Public Security Bureau's interrogation of the two suspects, Yang and Bao, before making a decision.

Hubei Refugees Accused of Robbery in Shanghai 121

Directors of Shaluo Township Accuse of Robbery　　Silver Notes Found in Refugees' Suitcases　　Police and Local Security Testify No Robbery　　Arguments Concluded, Awaiting Sentencing. Over two hundred refugees from Chun County, Hubei Province, which had suffered from the scourge of the Communists, elected Chen Zichun as their leader to represent them in requesting relief in various counties and cities. This group of refugees arrived in Shaluo Township, about five li southwest of Zhuanqiao in the southwestern township of this county. He Runzhi and He Xu, directors of the area, reported to the county public security bureau with Wang Chengyao, the head of the security team, and the refugee leaders Chen Zichun, Chen Hanxing, Chen Wangshi, and Chen Huangshi were detained. According to He Runzhi, the refugees had forcibly robbed them of over two hundred yuan in foreign currency, gold jewelry, eighty pairs of ivory chopsticks, and dozens of bolts of cloth. Subsequently, Captain Wang opened the refugees' suitcases and found 105 yuan in banknotes and 45 yuan in silver coins, but no jewelry, ivory, or cloth. The case was then transferred to the District Court, and Prosecutor Zhao prosecuted the refugees on charges of robbery. Yesterday morning, Judge Deng held a hearing. According to the refugees, they were not starving people, but prosperous citizens in their hometowns who had been harmed by the bandits and Communists and had come out to escape. Not one of the over two hundred people was without money. The banknotes that were found were their own and the travel expenses given by the institutions along the way, and the gold jewelry was also their own. From Zhuanqiao to the road, they were escorted out of the territory by patrol officers. If they had committed robbery, the police would never have allowed it. They also met the local security officer He Runyu, who distributed food and led them to the plaintiff's home. The plaintiff even paid them five yuan, which shows that they did not commit robbery. They also stated that the entire group is now working and waiting for the outcome of the case at Gaomiaozi in Pudong and requested a clear understanding. When questioned, the plaintiffs He Runzhi and his wife stated that the robbery was real and pointed to Chen Hanxing, Chen Wangshi, and Chen Huangshi as the perpetrators. Chen Zichun did not come. They also stated that there is now a pair of cloth pants that are stolen goods. The defendants stated that they saw a pair of white-waisted pants in the Public Security Bureau, but now they have a black cloth waist, which is a swap. The judge then summoned the security team leader Wang Chengyao, who testified that the defendants had committed robbery. However, the patrol officers Liu Desheng and He Yangfeng, who escorted them at the time, testified that they did not see them robbing. They were escorted in the back. According to Gu Xiaodi, who watched the Chun Shen Temple in Xinzhuang, he was the boatman who hired a boat for the refugees. The boatman Gu Caisheng stated that the refugees got on the boat and went to Maqiao without going ashore. The judge asked patrol officer Wang Zhiqiang, who testified that Wang Chengyao went to the refugees' place. The suitcases were locked, and Wang Chengyao opened the suitcases. The local security officer He Runyu testified that he distributed food but did not see them robbing. At this point, Prosecutor Zhao argued that it was clear that the case was real because the refugees had banknotes and gold jewelry. He requested that the defendants be sentenced according to law. The defendant's lawyer, Hu Yuanjun, argued that the defendants had been falsely accused and demanded that they be acquitted and released so that the entire group of over two hundred people could seek food. After reviewing the evidence, the judge ordered the arguments to be concluded and sentenced on the 24th. The defendants were remanded to custody.

Joint Report by the Public Security Bureau, Social Affairs Bureau, and Public Utilities Bureau on the Gaochang Temple Incident 123

Regarding the incident that occurred at Gaochang Temple between workers of the Chinese Electric Tram Company and workers of the Naval Aviation Department, the Public Security Bureau, Social Affairs Bureau, and Public Utilities Bureau were ordered by the Municipal Government to thoroughly investigate the situation at the time in order to clarify the truth. The investigation has now been completed, and a joint report was submitted to the mayor yesterday. The original report stated: "In response to the order from the secretary of the government, No. 1181, which instructed the bureaus to jointly investigate the conflict between the naval aviation drivers of the Naval Headquarters and the workers of the Shanghai Chinese Electric Tram Company, clarify the cause of the incident, and facilitate investigation, the Public Utilities Bureau dispatched technician Wu Jinhai, the Public Security Bureau dispatched clerk Chen Timin, and the Social Affairs Bureau dispatched investigator Zhu Guilin to the scene of the incident and various relevant places to conduct separate investigations. According to reports, the cause of the incident was that eleven workers from the Naval Aviation Department, including Zhang Likang, returned from Bansongyuan to Gaochang Temple, but the tram workers had already changed shifts. The reason for the beating is unknown. It is speculated that it may be related to the events of the day." Based on this, the tram workers in the Gaochang Temple area were beaten. According to the Zou patrol officer stationed there by the Public Security Bureau, this is a common occurrence, and not only are there no punitive measures after the tram workers are beaten, but the company often has to send free tickets. It seems that such a situation may not be a distant cause of the incident. The bureaus believe that as many as five people were injured in this incident. If no proper remedial measures are taken, the protection of tram workers will be non-existent. If there is a cycle of group fights and revenge, the consequences will be dire. In accordance with the above instructions, a copy of the investigation report and a copy of the vehicle damage list are attached. A joint report is submitted, requesting the Mayor to review and handle it for the public good. This report is drafted by the Social Affairs Bureau, and a joint statement is made for joint signature, which is inappropriate for printing separately. Respectfully submitted to Mayor Zhang.

Prohibition of Curing Diseases with Talismans 124

Notice from the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau. Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau issued a notice stating that curing diseases with talismans not only endangers human lives but also violates legal prohibitions. The Bureau has repeatedly issued strict notices to prohibit such practices. Completion of the Qingning Temple Floating Pier for City Ferries 125

Officially in Use Starting Yesterday. The Qingning Temple pier for the city-run Pujiang ferries was originally a reinforced concrete structure that was ten years old. Since the new steel-hulled ferries have been in operation, its lack of elasticity has caused damage to the pier with each docking due to the surge of waves, and many cement piles have been damaged. Moreover, the fixed pier cannot rise and fall with the tide, making it inconvenient for passengers to board and disembark. In order to permanently solve this problem, the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau cooperated with the Public Works Bureau to build a steel floating pier. It is reported that the project has been completed, and the city ferries began docking at the new pier yesterday (the 18th). There is a steel shed above to shelter from wind and rain, and the men's and women's restrooms all use flushing toilets. There is also a consumer cooperative where passengers can conveniently purchase sundries or exchange silver coins. It can be said to be a perfect match with the new ferries. It is reported that the cost is over 35,000 yuan.

Consumers' Cooperative of Civilian Residences 127

Preparatory Committee Established. The residents of the Shanghai Municipal Government's civilian residences are mostly coolies and slum dwellers whose livelihoods are very difficult. Wang Zhenchang, the general manager of the residence, has realized this and provided practical training and guidance to the residents on their livelihoods. Because the coolies' lives are poor, he sought comrades to initiate the organization of the Shanghai Municipal Civilian Residence Consumers' Cooperative. The spirit of this consumer cooperative is to solve the residents' livelihoods and improve their lives. It is reported that he has been approved by the Social Affairs Bureau and has received instructions from the Bureau to urge him to quickly and comprehensively plan and provide practical guidance to seek the happiness of the residents. When he initially announced the cooperative, the residents joined the cooperative enthusiastically. It is reported that he has already obtained more than twenty founding members and established the preparatory committee of the cooperative on the 13th of this month. He selected staff and actively conducted publicity among the residents. It is also reported that the preparatory committee of the cooperative held its first standing committee meeting yesterday, attended by more than thirty members, including Liu Wanyi. The general manager of the residence explained the main points of the consumer cooperative and guided the organization of the consumer cooperative. It is reported that the residents of the residence are very supportive of the establishment of the cooperative.

YWCA Memorial Hall 128

Commemorating Meritorious Women. In the memorial hall of the new YWCA building, all women who have contributed to the YWCA movement in China will be commemorated in the new building of the National Association of the YWCA on Yuanmingyuan Road, to commemorate their contributions. The woman who has made the greatest contribution to the Chinese YWCA is Ms. Gu Enci. She served as the first secretary of the Shanghai YWCA and then served as the general secretary of the National Association for many years. Her policy was to cultivate Chinese leaders to be able to undertake the work of the Chinese YWCA. She had a great foresight, and her value has become more apparent after her death. The seventh auditorium of the new building will be named Sigu Hall. All funds previously donated to commemorate Ms. Gu will be used to construct the hall. The auditorium is located in the northwest corner of the building, and its style is modeled after Chinese temples without adopting Western architecture. The teak and ceiling are also in the Chinese style. Mrs. John Bao passed away last year. The YWCA has now accepted the recommendation of Bao's donor to use the funds to purchase equipment in front of the auditorium, including offering tables, screens, and lecterns, as a memorial. In 1917, Ms. Mei Da of the United States donated funds to the YWCA's Girls' Physical Education Normal School at the time. Later, the school was merged into Jinling Women's University. In 1930, Ms. Da returned to China and greatly praised the construction of the new YWCA building and agreed to allocate the funds previously donated to the construction cost of the new building. The original intention of her previous donation was to commemorate her deceased daughter, Ms. Hamilton Da, so a monument will be erected in the new building to commemorate her permanently. Recently, Ms. Hua Jingxia's mother, Mrs. Hua, passed away in New York. Mrs. Hua served as the general secretary of the Shanghai YWCA and then devoted herself to training Chinese staff. She planned to return to China in 1928 to continue her work, but she was unable to do so due to poor health. Unexpectedly, the sad news came that Mrs. Hua had passed away in February. The association, in memory of her past efforts, will leave a memorial for Mrs. Hua in the new building.

Robbed of 500 Yuan, Two Fingers Cut Off 131

Wu Yunzhou's Encounter　　The Robbers Are Too Ruthless. Wu Yunzhou from Chuansha, Pudong, has always been a cloth broker. The other day, a certain cloth shop in the North City entrusted him to go to Nanhui, Pudong, to handle cloth. When he obtained 500 yuan, Wu crossed the river in the afternoon and went to the eastern township of Siza灶 when he was suddenly stopped by several bandits who robbed him of the 500 yuan he was carrying. Wu resisted and refused to let go. The bandits cut him on the back, the back of his hand, and his fingers with a knife, cutting off two fingers. Education News Headlines

Reassignment of the Tsinghua University President 145

New President Wu Nanxuan: Luo Jialun, President of National Tsinghua University, submitted his resignation, which was approved yesterday at the 16th State Council meeting. Wu Nanxuan was appointed as the President of Tsinghua University. The following is an exploration of the process of changing the university's president:

The Process of President Luo's Resignation: Since last year, Mr. Luo repeatedly submitted his resignation, but he was persuaded to stay. Later, the Central Government appointed Mr. Luo as the Director of Academic Affairs of the Central Political School and concurrently as the Acting Director of Education. Mr. Luo submitted his resignation again on January 22nd. At that time, the educational authorities believed that Mr. Luo had been working tirelessly to manage Tsinghua and actively rectify the situation, which was a fact. The government emphasized education and the rectification of academic atmosphere, and could not allow him to resign. However, since the Central Government had already decided to appoint him to an important position at the Central Political School, his determination to leave was firm. Therefore, they began to look for a successor, and on March 10th, they prepared a proposal and sent it to the Executive Yuan for submission to the State Council meeting. It happened that the meeting on that day was to commemorate the fallen soldiers, so the State Council meeting did not discuss it. It has now been formally approved by the State Council meeting yesterday. The Ministry of Education also issued an order approving Mr. Luo's resignation, as follows: "Since taking office as the President of the university, he has been dedicated to rectifying the situation, working tirelessly, and achieving remarkable results, which are highly valued. Now, according to his report, he has been ordered to preside over the academic affairs of the Central Political School and cannot go north. His request for resignation should be approved. In addition to submitting it to the State Council meeting for approval of his resignation and appointing another president to succeed him, he should be notified accordingly."

Selection and Brief Biography of the New President: The new president, Wu Nanxuan, who was appointed by the State Council meeting yesterday, was carefully selected and personally decided by Jiang, who also serves as the Minister. Mr. Wu's original name is [blank space] from Yizheng, Jiangsu. He holds a Bachelor of Arts, Master's degree, and Doctorate in Education from the University of California, USA. He has served as a translator in the Agricultural Department of the US government, the chief editor of the Young China Morning Post in San Francisco, USA, and a professor at Lincoln University for 18 years. In April of the 18th year, he was dispatched by the Ministry of Education to inspect education in the United States. In November of the 18th year, he returned to China and served as the Deputy Director of Academic Affairs of the Central Political School, a specialized member of the Examination Committee of the Examination Yuan, and a member of the Central Government's Committee for the Management of Students Studying Abroad. He is highly regarded for his extensive academic knowledge and experience, as well as his dedication and diligence.

Ministry of Education Meets with Students: Students from the university elected representatives to come to Beijing to request the prompt appointment of a president. The Ministry of Education had previously telegraphed the university's school affairs meeting to inform them that the selection of the president would be decided soon and instructed them to inform the students that there was no need to come to Beijing. Later, three students from the university, Liu Hanwen, Lin Wenguang, and Wang Su, came to Beijing to personally present a document to the Ministry, stating that the government has the authority to weigh the appointment of the president of a national university, and students should focus on their studies and not interfere excessively. The students went to the Ministry a few days ago and Deputy Minister Chen explained this to the students in detail. Yesterday, Chairman Jiang also summoned the students to give them personal instructions.

Anhui Provincial Government Persuades Anhui University President to Stay 146

During the sick leave period, Vice President Ding Xuxian will act on behalf of the president. A new president will be selected after the new Director of Education arrives. Anhui University President Yang Lianggong submitted his resignation to the provincial government due to repeated campus unrest and went to Shanghai for medical treatment. The provost, Chang Daozhi, is acting as president. The provincial government's 179th regular meeting on the 13th discussed Yang's resignation and decided to persuade him to stay during his medical treatment. During the period of medical leave, Vice President Ding Xuxian will temporarily act as president. It is reported that Yang still needs to resign again. The selection of a new president will be determined after the new Director of Education arrives in Anhui. At this time, no one in the Department of Education is responsible, and they have no choice but to put this major issue aside for the time being.

Ministry of Education Bans Two Films 147

"The Terrifying Impermanence" and "The Romantic Monk": Yesterday, the Ministry of Education issued a notice to the Social Affairs Bureaus and Education Bureaus of Shanghai and other cities (except Nanjing), the Civil Affairs Departments and Education Departments of various provinces, and the Weihaiwei Management Office, stating: "It is approved that the Nanjing Municipal Government's consultation states that the Social Affairs and Education Bureaus submitted that the films 'The Terrifying Impermanence' and 'The Romantic Monk' violate the provisions of the review standards and asked whether to issue a nationwide ban and destroy the negatives. After investigation, since the film is a performance of superstition and obscenity, violating laws and regulations, it should be banned by a general order. In addition to replying to the Nanjing Municipal Government to instruct the Social Affairs and Education Bureaus to destroy the negatives and order a separate ban, it is hereby copied and ordered to be obeyed and to instruct all subordinates to obey and strictly ban it in order to maintain morality. This order."
